NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING 
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES 
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER 
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By  Order)
Commissioner  of  Stationery  and  Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICES
 
Arockia Aswina P, a female child born to Thiru Peter I, on 12th May 1996 residing at No.12-288, Anna Nagar,
Vadakkankulam, Perungudi, Tirunelveli-627 116, has been living as male after an elaborate sexual reassignment surgery
by Dr. Meghna S Bagalkotkar Tamil Nadu Medical Council, Mahatma Gandhi Hospital, Pondicherry-607 402. By this I may be 
treated as male and shall henceforth be known as HARISH P.
Tirunelveli, 
P. AROCKIA ASWINA
18th February 2021.
